FILE: src\ProjectName.AppHost\AppHost.cs

using CommunityToolkit.Aspire.Hosting.Ollama;

var builder = DistributedApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

// ============================================================================
// INFRASTRUCTURE
// ============================================================================

var redis = builder.AddRedis("redis").WithDataVolume();

// PostgreSQL with pgvector for RAG Knowledge Vault
var knowledgeDb = builder.AddPostgres("knowledge-db")
    .WithImage("pgvector/pgvector", "pg16")
    .WithDataVolume()
    .WithPgAdmin()
    .AddDatabase("knowledge");

// Ollama LLM Server with GPU support
var ollama = builder.AddOllama("ollama", port: 11434)
    .WithDataVolume()
    .WithLifetime(ContainerLifetime.Persistent)
    .WithContainerRuntimeArgs("--gpus=all") // Enable NVIDIA GPU passthrough
    .WithEnvironment("OLLAMA_NUM_GPU", "1");

// ============================================================================
// LLM MODELS - The Council
// ============================================================================

var llama = ollama.AddModel("qwen2.5-coder:7b"); // The Coder - Better tool-calling compliance
var phi = ollama.AddModel("phi3"); // The Creative/Cheap Agent
var trained = ollama.AddModel("llama3.2-finetuned"); // The Expert/Trained Agent (Self-Trained)
var embeddings = ollama.AddModel("nomic-embed-text"); // Embedding Model for RAG

// PMCR-O Agent Services
var planner = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_PlannerService>("planner-agent")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

var maker = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_MakerService>("maker-agent")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

var checker = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_CheckerService>("checker-agent")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

var reflector = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_ReflectorService>("reflector-agent")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

var orchestrator = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_OrchestratorService>("orchestrator-agent")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

// AI Engine Service (Fine-tuning & Model Management)
var aiEngine = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_AIEngine>("ai-engine")
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(llama);

// Knowledge Service (RAG - Vector Search & Memory)
var knowledgeService = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_KnowledgeService>("knowledge-service")
    .WithReference(knowledgeDb)
    .WithReference(ollama)
    .WaitFor(knowledgeDb)
    .WaitFor(embeddings);

// Orchestration API (REST Gateway)
var orchestrationApi = builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_OrchestrationApi>("orchestration-api")
    .WithReference(planner)
    .WithReference(maker)
    .WithReference(checker)
    .WithReference(reflector)
    .WithReference(orchestrator)
    .WithReference(knowledgeService)
    .WithReference(ollama); // Required for OllamaTestController to get connection string

// PMCR-O Dashboard (Telerik Blazor)
builder.AddProject<Projects.ProjectName_Dashboard>("dashboard")
    .WithReference(orchestrationApi)
    .WithExternalHttpEndpoints();

builder.Build().Run();

using System.Net.Http;
using System.Threading;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.Kestrel.Core;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http.Resilience;
using OllamaSharp;
using ProjectName.CheckerService.Services;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.AddServiceDefaults();
builder.Services.AddGrpc();

// Configure Kestrel for HTTP/2 (required for gRPC over non-TLS)
builder.WebHost.ConfigureKestrel(options =>
{
    options.ConfigureEndpointDefaults(listenOptions =>
    {
        listenOptions.Protocols = HttpProtocols.Http2;
    });
});

// Ollama Setup
var ollamaUri = builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("ollama") 
    ?? "http://localhost:11434";
var modelId = "qwen2.5-coder:7b";

if (!Uri.TryCreate(ollamaUri, UriKind.Absolute, out var uri))
{
    uri = new Uri("http://localhost:11434");
}

// Register HttpClient for Ollama
builder.Services.AddHttpClient("ollama", client =>
{
    client.BaseAddress = uri;
    client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
})
.ConfigurePrimaryHttpMessageHandler(() => new SocketsHttpHandler
{
    ConnectTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30),
    PooledConnectionLifetime = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10),
    PooledConnectionIdleTimeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)
})
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// ‚úÖ CRITICAL FIX: Register IChatClient with UseFunctionInvocation middleware
builder.Services.AddSingleton<IChatClient>(sp =>
{
    var httpClient = sp.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>().CreateClient("ollama");
    var baseClient = new OllamaApiClient(httpClient, modelId);
    
    return new ChatClientBuilder(baseClient)
        .UseFunctionInvocation() // ‚úÖ Critical middleware
        .Build();
});

// Register MCP Tools Helper (shared)
builder.Services.AddSingleton<ProjectName.Shared.Services.AgentMcpToolsHelper>();
builder.Services.AddSingleton<McpToolsHelper>();

var app = builder.Build();

app.MapDefaultEndpoints();
app.MapGrpcService<CheckerAgentService>();
app.MapGet("/", () => "PMCR-O Checker Agent Service - gRPC endpoint available");

app.Run();

FILE: src\ProjectName.CheckerService\Services\CheckerAgentService.cs
================================================================================

using Grpc.Core;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using OllamaSharp;
using ProjectName.CheckerService.Services;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.CheckerService.Services;

public class CheckerAgentService : AgentService.AgentServiceBase
{
    private readonly IChatClient _chatClient;
    private readonly ILoggerFactory _loggerFactory;
    private readonly ILogger<CheckerAgentService> _logger;
    private readonly McpToolsHelper _mcpToolsHelper;
    private readonly IPromptManager _promptManager;

    public CheckerAgentService(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        ILogger<CheckerAgentService> logger,
        McpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        IPromptManager promptManager)
    {
        _chatClient = chatClient;
        _loggerFactory = loggerFactory;
        _logger = logger;
        _mcpToolsHelper = mcpToolsHelper;
        _promptManager = promptManager;
    }

    public override async Task<AgentResponse> ExecuteTask(
        AgentRequest request,
        ServerCallContext context)
    {
        _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ I am the Checker. I am validating: {Intent}", request.Intent);

        try
        {
            // Get MCP tools for the Checker (Playwright, etc.)
            var mcpTools = await _mcpToolsHelper.GetCheckerToolsAsync();

            // Create agent using Microsoft.Agents.AI with MCP tools
            var agent = new ChatClientAgent(
                _chatClient,
                new ChatClientAgentOptions
                {
                    Name = "Checker",
                    Description = "Quality Assurance Checker for PMCR-O system",
                    ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                    {
                        Instructions = _promptManager.GetPrompt("checker"),
                        Tools = mcpTools
                    }
                },
                _loggerFactory);

            // Execute the checking task
            var thread = agent.GetNewThread();
            var response = await agent.RunAsync(
                new Microsoft.Extensions.AI.ChatMessage(
                    Microsoft.Extensions.AI.ChatRole.User,
                    request.Intent),
                thread);

            var validationContent = response.Text ?? "[No validation performed]";

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ I have completed my validation phase. Errors parsed and formatted.");

            return new AgentResponse
            {
                Content = validationContent,
                Success = true
            };
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Checker failed for intent: {Intent}", request.Intent);
            return new AgentResponse
            {
                Content = $"Checker error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            };
        }
    }
}

using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.CheckerService.Services;

/// <summary>
/// Legacy helper - now uses shared AgentMcpToolsHelper
/// Kept for backward compatibility
/// </summary>
public class McpToolsHelper
{
    private readonly AgentMcpToolsHelper _sharedHelper;

    public McpToolsHelper(AgentMcpToolsHelper sharedHelper)
    {
        _sharedHelper = sharedHelper;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Creates MCP tools for the Checker agent (e.g., Playwright for browser testing)
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<List<Microsoft.Extensions.AI.AITool>> GetCheckerToolsAsync()
    {
        return await _sharedHelper.GetCheckerToolsAsync();
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Dashboard\Controllers\CultureController.cs

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Localization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;

[Route("[controller]/[action]")]
public class CultureController : Controller
{
    public IActionResult Set(string culture, string redirectUri)
    {
        if (culture != null)
        {
            HttpContext.Response.Cookies.Append(
                CookieRequestCultureProvider.DefaultCookieName,
                CookieRequestCultureProvider.MakeCookieValue(
                    new RequestCulture(culture, culture)));
        }

        return LocalRedirect(redirectUri);
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Dashboard\Program.cs

using ProjectName.Dashboard.Components;
using ProjectName.Dashboard.Services;
using Telerik.Blazor.Services;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.AddServiceDefaults();

builder.Services.AddTelerikBlazor();
builder.Services.AddSignalR();
builder.Services.AddHttpClient();

#region Localization
builder.Services.AddControllers();
builder.Services.AddSingleton(typeof(ITelerikStringLocalizer), typeof(ResxLocalizer));
builder.Services.AddLocalization(options => options.ResourcesPath = "Resources");
#endregion Localization

// Add services to the container.
builder.Services.AddRazorComponents()
    .AddInteractiveServerComponents();

var app = builder.Build();

// Configure the HTTP request pipeline.
if (!app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseExceptionHandler("/Error", createScopeForErrors: true);
    // The default HSTS value is 30 days. You may want to change this for production scenarios, see https://aka.ms/aspnetcore-hsts.
    app.UseHsts();
}

app.UseStatusCodePagesWithReExecute("/not-found", createScopeForStatusCodePages: true);
app.UseHttpsRedirection();

app.MapStaticAssets();
app.UseAntiforgery();

var supportedCultures = new[] { "en-US", "de-DE", "es-ES", "bg-BG" };
var localizationOptions = new RequestLocalizationOptions()
    .SetDefaultCulture(supportedCultures[0])
    .AddSupportedCultures(supportedCultures)
    .AddSupportedUICultures(supportedCultures);

app.UseRequestLocalization(localizationOptions);

app.MapControllers();

// SignalR Hub for real-time cognitive trail
app.MapHub<CognitiveTrailHub>("/hubs/cognitive-trail");

app.MapRazorComponents<App>()
    .AddInteractiveServerRenderMode();

app.Run();

FILE: src\ProjectName.Dashboard\Services\CognitiveTrailHub.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.Client;

namespace ProjectName.Dashboard.Services;

/// <summary>
/// SignalR Hub for real-time Cognitive Trail updates
/// The Strange Loop's neural pathway - thoughts flow through here
/// </summary>
public class CognitiveTrailHub : Hub
{
    public async Task BroadcastThought(string agent, string message, string cycleId)
    {
        await Clients.All.SendAsync("ReceiveThought", new
        {
            Timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("HH:mm:ss"),
            Agent = agent,
            Message = message,
            CycleId = cycleId
        });
    }

    public async Task BroadcastLoopState(string activeNode, int iterationCount)
    {
        await Clients.All.SendAsync("LoopStateChanged", new
        {
            ActiveNode = activeNode,
            IterationCount = iterationCount,
            Timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow
        });
    }

    public override async Task OnConnectedAsync()
    {
        await Clients.Caller.SendAsync("Connected", $"Observer connected to Strange Loop at {DateTime.UtcNow}");
        await base.OnConnectedAsync();
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Client service for components to interact with the hub
/// </summary>
public class CognitiveTrailHubService : IAsyncDisposable
{
    private readonly HubConnection? _hubConnection;
    
    public event Action<TrailUpdate>? OnTrailUpdate;
    public event Action<LoopState>? OnLoopStateChanged;

    public CognitiveTrailHubService(NavigationManager navigationManager)
    {
        _hubConnection = new HubConnectionBuilder()
            .WithUrl(navigationManager.ToAbsoluteUri("/hubs/cognitive-trail"))
            .WithAutomaticReconnect()
            .Build();

        _hubConnection.On<TrailUpdate>("ReceiveThought", update =>
        {
            OnTrailUpdate?.Invoke(update);
        });

        _hubConnection.On<LoopState>("LoopStateChanged", state =>
        {
            OnLoopStateChanged?.Invoke(state);
        });
    }

    public async Task StartAsync()
    {
        if (_hubConnection?.State == HubConnectionState.Disconnected)
        {
            await _hubConnection.StartAsync();
        }
    }

    public async Task SendIntentAsync(string intent)
    {
        if (_hubConnection is not null)
        {
            await _hubConnection.SendAsync("ProcessIntent", intent);
        }
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        if (_hubConnection is not null)
        {
            await _hubConnection.DisposeAsync();
        }
    }

    public record TrailUpdate(string Timestamp, string Agent, string Message, string CycleId);
    public record LoopState(string ActiveNode, int IterationCount, DateTime Timestamp);
}

using ProjectName.Dashboard.Resources;

        {
            get

            }

            return TelerikMessages.ResourceManager.GetString(key, TelerikMessages.Culture) ?? string.Empty;
        }
    }

FILE: src\ProjectName.KnowledgeService\Controllers\KnowledgeController.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Services;

namespace ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API for the Knowledge Vault (RAG)
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
public class KnowledgeController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly KnowledgeVaultService _knowledgeVault;
    private readonly ILogger<KnowledgeController> _logger;

    public KnowledgeController(
        KnowledgeVaultService knowledgeVault,
        ILogger<KnowledgeController> logger)
    {
        _knowledgeVault = knowledgeVault;
        _logger = logger;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Ingest new knowledge into the vault
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost("ingest")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<IngestResponse>> Ingest([FromBody] IngestRequest request)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(request.Content))
        {
            return BadRequest("Content is required");
        }

        _logger.LogInformation("üì• Ingesting knowledge: {Preview}...", 
            request.Content.Length > 50 ? request.Content[..50] : request.Content);

        var entry = await _knowledgeVault.IngestAsync(
            request.Content,
            request.Source,
            request.Category,
            request.Metadata);

        return Ok(new IngestResponse
        {
            Id = entry.Id,
            Message = "Knowledge ingested successfully",
            CreatedAt = entry.CreatedAt
        });
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Retrieve relevant knowledge based on a query
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost("retrieve")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<RetrieveResponse>> Retrieve([FromBody] RetrieveRequest request)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(request.Query))
        {
            return BadRequest("Query is required");
        }

        _logger.LogInformation("üîç Searching knowledge vault for: {Query}", request.Query);

        var results = await _knowledgeVault.RetrieveAsync(
            request.Query,
            request.TopK ?? 5,
            request.Category,
            request.MinSimilarity ?? 0.5f);

        return Ok(new RetrieveResponse
        {
            Query = request.Query,
            Results = results.Select(r => new RetrieveResult
            {
                Id = r.Entry.Id,
                Content = r.Entry.Content,
                Source = r.Entry.Source,
                Category = r.Entry.Category,
                Similarity = r.Similarity,
                CreatedAt = r.Entry.CreatedAt
            }).ToList(),
            TotalFound = results.Count
        });
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Get knowledge vault statistics
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("stats")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<KnowledgeVaultStats>> GetStats()
    {
        var stats = await _knowledgeVault.GetStatsAsync();
        return Ok(stats);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Delete a knowledge entry
    /// </summary>
    [HttpDelete("{id:guid}")]
    public async Task<ActionResult> Delete(Guid id)
    {
        var deleted = await _knowledgeVault.DeleteAsync(id);
        if (!deleted)
        {
            return NotFound();
        }
        return NoContent();
    }
}

// Request/Response DTOs

public class IngestRequest
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string? Source { get; set; }
    public string? Category { get; set; }
    public string? Metadata { get; set; }
}

public class IngestResponse
{
    public Guid Id { get; set; }
    public string Message { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; }
}

public class RetrieveRequest
{
    public string Query { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public int? TopK { get; set; }
    public string? Category { get; set; }
    public float? MinSimilarity { get; set; }
}

public class RetrieveResponse
{
    public string Query { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public List<RetrieveResult> Results { get; set; } = new();
    public int TotalFound { get; set; }
}

public class RetrieveResult
{
    public Guid Id { get; set; }
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string? Source { get; set; }
    public string? Category { get; set; }
    public float Similarity { get; set; }
    public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.KnowledgeService\Data\KnowledgeDbContext.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using Pgvector;
using Pgvector.EntityFrameworkCore;

namespace ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Data;

/// <summary>
/// Entity Framework DbContext for the Knowledge Vault (RAG storage)
/// </summary>
public class KnowledgeDbContext : DbContext
{
    public KnowledgeDbContext(DbContextOptions<KnowledgeDbContext> options) : base(options)
    {
    }

    public DbSet<KnowledgeEntry> KnowledgeEntries { get; set; } = null!;

    protected override void OnModelCreating(ModelBuilder modelBuilder)
    {
        base.OnModelCreating(modelBuilder);

        // Enable pgvector extension
        modelBuilder.HasPostgresExtension("vector");

        modelBuilder.Entity<KnowledgeEntry>(entity =>
        {
            entity.HasKey(e => e.Id);
            entity.Property(e => e.Id).ValueGeneratedOnAdd();
            
            // Vector column for embeddings (1024 dimensions for nomic-embed-text)
            entity.Property(e => e.Embedding)
                .HasColumnType("vector(768)"); // nomic-embed-text uses 768 dimensions
            
            entity.Property(e => e.Content).IsRequired();
            entity.Property(e => e.Source).HasMaxLength(500);
            entity.Property(e => e.Category).HasMaxLength(100);
            
            // Index for vector similarity search
            entity.HasIndex(e => e.Embedding)
                .HasMethod("ivfflat")
                .HasOperators("vector_cosine_ops")
                .HasStorageParameter("lists", 100);
        });
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// A knowledge entry stored in the vector database
/// </summary>
public class KnowledgeEntry
{
    public Guid Id { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// The original text content
    /// </summary>
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    
    /// <summary>
    /// Vector embedding of the content (768 dimensions for nomic-embed-text)
    /// </summary>
    public Vector? Embedding { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// Source of the knowledge (e.g., "workflow_log", "user_input", "documentation")
    /// </summary>
    public string? Source { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// Category for filtering (e.g., "error_pattern", "solution", "code_snippet")
    /// </summary>
    public string? Category { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// Additional metadata as JSON
    /// </summary>
    public string? Metadata { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// When this knowledge was ingested
    /// </summary>
    public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
    
    /// <summary>
    /// Last time this knowledge was accessed/used
    /// </summary>
    public DateTime? LastAccessedAt { get; set; }
    
    /// <summary>
    /// How many times this knowledge has been retrieved
    /// </summary>
    public int AccessCount { get; set; } = 0;
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.KnowledgeService\Program.cs

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using OllamaSharp;
using ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Data;
using ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Services;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

// Add service defaults (logging, OpenTelemetry, etc.)
builder.AddServiceDefaults();

// PostgreSQL with pgvector (Aspire provides connection string as "knowledge")
var connectionString = builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("knowledge") 
    ?? builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("knowledge-db")
    ?? "Host=localhost;Database=knowledge;Username=postgres;Password=postgres";

Console.WriteLine($"üì¶ Knowledge DB Connection: {connectionString}");

builder.Services.AddDbContext<KnowledgeDbContext>(options =>
    options.UseNpgsql(connectionString, npgsqlOptions =>
    {
        npgsqlOptions.UseVector();
    }));

// Ollama for embeddings
var ollamaUri = builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("ollama") 
    ?? "http://localhost:11434";

if (!Uri.TryCreate(ollamaUri, UriKind.Absolute, out var uri))
{
    uri = new Uri("http://localhost:11434");
}

builder.Services.AddSingleton(_ => new OllamaApiClient(uri));
builder.Services.AddScoped<EmbeddingService>();
builder.Services.AddScoped<KnowledgeVaultService>();

// Add controllers
builder.Services.AddControllers();
builder.Services.AddEndpointsApiExplorer();
builder.Services.AddSwaggerGen();

var app = builder.Build();

// Configure the HTTP request pipeline
app.MapDefaultEndpoints();

if (app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseSwagger();
    app.UseSwaggerUI();
}

app.MapControllers();

// Initialize database
using (var scope = app.Services.CreateScope())
{
    var db = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService<KnowledgeDbContext>();
    try
    {
        await db.Database.MigrateAsync();
    }
    catch
    {
        // If migrations fail, try to ensure created (for initial setup)
        await db.Database.EnsureCreatedAsync();
    }
}

app.MapGet("/", () => "PMCR-O Knowledge Service - RAG Vector Database");

app.Run();

FILE: src\ProjectName.KnowledgeService\Services\EmbeddingService.cs
================================================================================

using OllamaSharp;
using Pgvector;

namespace ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Services;

/// <summary>
/// Service for generating embeddings using Ollama
/// </summary>
public class EmbeddingService
{
    private readonly OllamaApiClient _ollama;
    private readonly ILogger<EmbeddingService> _logger;
    private const string EmbeddingModel = "nomic-embed-text";

    public EmbeddingService(OllamaApiClient ollama, ILogger<EmbeddingService> logger)
    {
        _ollama = ollama;
        _logger = logger;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Generate an embedding vector for the given text
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<Vector> GenerateEmbeddingAsync(string text)
    {
        _logger.LogDebug("Generating embedding for text of length {Length}", text.Length);

        try
        {
            var response = await _ollama.EmbedAsync(new OllamaSharp.Models.EmbedRequest
            {
                Model = EmbeddingModel,
                Input = [text]
            });

            if (response?.Embeddings == null || response.Embeddings.Count == 0)
            {
                throw new InvalidOperationException("Ollama returned empty embeddings");
            }

            var embedding = response.Embeddings[0];
            _logger.LogDebug("Generated embedding with {Dimensions} dimensions", embedding.Length);

            return new Vector(embedding.Select(x => (float)x).ToArray());
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "Failed to generate embedding");
            throw;
        }
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Generate embeddings for multiple texts in batch
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<List<Vector>> GenerateEmbeddingsAsync(IEnumerable<string> texts)
    {
        var textList = texts.ToList();
        _logger.LogDebug("Generating embeddings for {Count} texts", textList.Count);

        var embeddings = new List<Vector>();

        foreach (var text in textList)
        {
            var embedding = await GenerateEmbeddingAsync(text);
            embeddings.Add(embedding);
        }

        return embeddings;
    }
}




================================================================================
FILE: src\ProjectName.KnowledgeService\Services\KnowledgeVaultService.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using Pgvector;
using Pgvector.EntityFrameworkCore;
using ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Data;

namespace ProjectName.KnowledgeService.Services;

/// <summary>
/// Service for managing the Knowledge Vault (RAG storage and retrieval)
/// </summary>
public class KnowledgeVaultService
{
    private readonly KnowledgeDbContext _db;
    private readonly EmbeddingService _embeddingService;
    private readonly ILogger<KnowledgeVaultService> _logger;

    public KnowledgeVaultService(
        KnowledgeDbContext db,
        EmbeddingService embeddingService,
        ILogger<KnowledgeVaultService> logger)
    {
        _db = db;
        _embeddingService = embeddingService;
        _logger = logger;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Ingest new knowledge into the vault
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<KnowledgeEntry> IngestAsync(
        string content,
        string? source = null,
        string? category = null,
        string? metadata = null)
    {
        _logger.LogInformation("üì• Ingesting knowledge: {Preview}...", 
            content.Length > 50 ? content[..50] : content);

        // Generate embedding
        var embedding = await _embeddingService.GenerateEmbeddingAsync(content);

        var entry = new KnowledgeEntry
        {
            Id = Guid.NewGuid(),
            Content = content,
            Embedding = embedding,
            Source = source,
            Category = category,
            Metadata = metadata,
            CreatedAt = DateTime.UtcNow
        };

        _db.KnowledgeEntries.Add(entry);
        await _db.SaveChangesAsync();

        _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Knowledge ingested with ID: {Id}", entry.Id);
        return entry;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Retrieve relevant knowledge based on a query
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<List<KnowledgeSearchResult>> RetrieveAsync(
        string query,
        int topK = 5,
        string? category = null,
        float minSimilarity = 0.5f)
    {
        _logger.LogInformation("üîç Searching knowledge vault for: {Query}", query);

        // Generate embedding for query
        var queryEmbedding = await _embeddingService.GenerateEmbeddingAsync(query);

        // Build query
        var dbQuery = _db.KnowledgeEntries.AsQueryable();

        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(category))
        {
            dbQuery = dbQuery.Where(e => e.Category == category);
        }

        // Perform vector similarity search using cosine distance
        var results = await dbQuery
            .Select(e => new
            {
                Entry = e,
                Distance = e.Embedding!.CosineDistance(queryEmbedding)
            })
            .OrderBy(x => x.Distance)
            .Take(topK)
            .ToListAsync();

        // Convert distance to similarity (1 - distance for cosine)
        var searchResults = results
            .Select(r => new KnowledgeSearchResult
            {
                Entry = r.Entry,
                Similarity = 1 - (float)r.Distance
            })
            .Where(r => r.Similarity >= minSimilarity)
            .ToList();

        // Update access counts
        foreach (var result in searchResults)
        {
            result.Entry.LastAccessedAt = DateTime.UtcNow;
            result.Entry.AccessCount++;
        }
        await _db.SaveChangesAsync();

        _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Found {Count} relevant knowledge entries", searchResults.Count);
        return searchResults;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Get knowledge entry by ID
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<KnowledgeEntry?> GetByIdAsync(Guid id)
    {
        return await _db.KnowledgeEntries.FindAsync(id);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Delete knowledge entry
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<bool> DeleteAsync(Guid id)
    {
        var entry = await _db.KnowledgeEntries.FindAsync(id);
        if (entry == null) return false;

        _db.KnowledgeEntries.Remove(entry);
        await _db.SaveChangesAsync();
        return true;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Get statistics about the knowledge vault
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<KnowledgeVaultStats> GetStatsAsync()
    {
        return new KnowledgeVaultStats
        {
            TotalEntries = await _db.KnowledgeEntries.CountAsync(),
            CategoriesCount = await _db.KnowledgeEntries
                .Where(e => e.Category != null)
                .Select(e => e.Category)
                .Distinct()
                .CountAsync(),
            SourcesCount = await _db.KnowledgeEntries
                .Where(e => e.Source != null)
                .Select(e => e.Source)
                .Distinct()
                .CountAsync(),
            MostAccessedEntries = await _db.KnowledgeEntries
                .OrderByDescending(e => e.AccessCount)
                .Take(5)
                .Select(e => new { e.Id, e.Content, e.AccessCount })
                .ToListAsync()
        };
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Result of a knowledge search
/// </summary>
public class KnowledgeSearchResult
{
    public KnowledgeEntry Entry { get; set; } = null!;
    public float Similarity { get; set; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Statistics about the knowledge vault
/// </summary>
public class KnowledgeVaultStats
{
    public int TotalEntries { get; set; }
    public int CategoriesCount { get; set; }
    public int SourcesCount { get; set; }
    public object? MostAccessedEntries { get; set; }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.MakerService\Program.cs

using System.Net.Http;
using System.Threading;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.Kestrel.Core;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http.Resilience;
using OllamaSharp;
using ProjectName.MakerService.Services;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.AddServiceDefaults();
builder.Services.AddGrpc();

// Configure Kestrel for HTTP/2 (required for gRPC over non-TLS)
builder.WebHost.ConfigureKestrel(options =>
{
    options.ConfigureEndpointDefaults(listenOptions =>
    {
        // Force HTTP/2 for gRPC to work over non-TLS connections
        // This matches Aspire's development environment behavior
        listenOptions.Protocols = HttpProtocols.Http2;
    });
});

// Ollama Setup - using Aspire connection string
var ollamaUri = builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("ollama") 
    ?? "http://localhost:11434";
var modelId = "qwen2.5-coder:7b";

if (!Uri.TryCreate(ollamaUri, UriKind.Absolute, out var uri))
{
    uri = new Uri("http://localhost:11434");
}

// Register HttpClient for Ollama with increased timeout
// CRITICAL: Increase timeout for LLM inference (especially on CPU)
// Default 10s is too short - LLMs can take 30s-2min on CPU
builder.Services.AddHttpClient("ollama", client =>
{
    client.BaseAddress = uri;
    // Set HttpClient timeout to infinite - let resilience handler control it
    client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
})
.ConfigurePrimaryHttpMessageHandler(() => new SocketsHttpHandler
{
    // Also set socket-level timeouts
    ConnectTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30),
    PooledConnectionLifetime = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10),
    PooledConnectionIdleTimeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)
})
// Override default resilience handler for LLM requests
// The standard resilience handler has a 10s timeout which is too short
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    // Increase attempt timeout for LLM inference (can take 30s-2min on CPU)
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    
    // Total request timeout (all retries combined)
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    
    // Reduce retry attempts for long-running operations
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    
    // Circuit breaker sampling duration must be at least double the attempt timeout
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// ‚úÖ CRITICAL FIX: Register IChatClient with UseFunctionInvocation middleware
// This middleware automatically:
// 1. Detects tool call JSON from Ollama's text response
// 2. Executes the tool functions
// 3. Returns results to the LLM
// 4. Continues the conversation until completion
builder.Services.AddSingleton<IChatClient>(sp =>
{
    var httpClient = sp.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>().CreateClient("ollama");
    var baseClient = new OllamaApiClient(httpClient, modelId);
    
    // üî• THE GOLDEN BRIDGE: UseFunctionInvocation() middleware
    var chatClient = new ChatClientBuilder(baseClient)
        .UseFunctionInvocation() // ‚úÖ This is the missing piece
        .Build();
    
    return chatClient;
});

// Register MCP Tools Helper (shared)
builder.Services.AddSingleton<ProjectName.Shared.Services.AgentMcpToolsHelper>();

var app = builder.Build();

app.MapDefaultEndpoints();
app.MapGrpcService<MakerAgentService>();
app.MapGet("/", () => "PMCR-O Maker Agent Service - gRPC endpoint available");

app.Run();

FILE: src\ProjectName.MakerService\Services\MakerAgentService.cs
================================================================================

using Grpc.Core;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using OllamaSharp;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.MakerService.Services;

public class MakerAgentService : AgentService.AgentServiceBase
{
    private readonly IChatClient _chatClient;
    private readonly ILoggerFactory _loggerFactory;
    private readonly ILogger<MakerAgentService> _logger;
    private readonly AgentMcpToolsHelper _mcpToolsHelper;
    private readonly IPromptManager _promptManager;

    public MakerAgentService(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        ILogger<MakerAgentService> logger,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        IPromptManager promptManager)
    {
        _chatClient = chatClient;
        _loggerFactory = loggerFactory;
        _logger = logger;
        _mcpToolsHelper = mcpToolsHelper;
        _promptManager = promptManager;
    }

    public override async Task<AgentResponse> ExecuteTask(
        AgentRequest request,
        ServerCallContext context)
    {
        _logger.LogInformation("üî® I am the Maker. I am executing the task: {Intent}", request.Intent);

        try
        {
            // Get MCP tools for the Maker (filesystem, terminal, etc.)
            var mcpTools = await _mcpToolsHelper.GetMakerToolsAsync();
            
            // Get native .NET tools (WriteFileDirect)
            var dotNetTools = CustomDotNetTools.GetMakerDotNetTools();
            
            // Combine all tools
            var allTools = new List<AITool>();
            allTools.AddRange(mcpTools);
            allTools.AddRange(dotNetTools);

            // Create agent using Microsoft.Agents.AI with native tool calling
            var agent = new ChatClientAgent(
                _chatClient,
                new ChatClientAgentOptions
                {
                    Name = "Maker",
                    Description = "Implementation Maker for PMCR-O system",
                    ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                    {
                        Instructions = _promptManager.GetPrompt("maker"),
                        Tools = allTools
                    }
                },
                _loggerFactory);

            // ENTERPRISE_UPGRADE: Execute with native function invocation
            // Microsoft.Agents.AI automatically handles tool execution when tools are provided in ChatOptions.Tools
            // The framework will detect tool calls in the LLM response and execute them automatically
            var thread = agent.GetNewThread();
            
            // Run the agent - the framework will automatically detect and execute tool calls
            var response = await agent.RunAsync(
                new Microsoft.Extensions.AI.ChatMessage(
                    Microsoft.Extensions.AI.ChatRole.User,
                    request.Intent),
                thread);

            var implementationContent = response.Text ?? "[No implementation generated]";
            
            // ENTERPRISE_UPGRADE: Native Function Invocation
            // Microsoft.Agents.AI automatically handles tool execution when tools are provided in ChatOptions.Tools
            // The framework will detect tool calls in the LLM response and execute them automatically
            // Tool results are included in the conversation context automatically
            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Agent execution completed. Tools were executed automatically by the framework if needed.");

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ I have completed my implementation phase. Code/artifacts generated.");

            return new AgentResponse
            {
                Content = implementationContent,
                Success = true
            };
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Maker failed for intent: {Intent}", request.Intent);
            return new AgentResponse
            {
                Content = $"Maker error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            };
        }
    }
}

using System;
using Grpc.Core;
using Grpc.Net.Client;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API controller for the Checker Agent Service
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Produces("application/json")]
public class CheckerController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ILogger<CheckerController> _logger;
    private readonly IServiceProvider _serviceProvider;

    public CheckerController(
        ILogger<CheckerController> logger,
        IServiceProvider serviceProvider)
    {
        _logger = logger;
        _serviceProvider = serviceProvider;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Execute a validation task via the Checker gRPC service
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="request">The validation request with implementation to check</param>
    /// <returns>The checker's response</returns>
    [HttpPost("check")]
    [ProducesResponseType(typeof(CheckerResponse), StatusCodes.Status200OK)]
    [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]
    public async Task<IActionResult> Check([FromBody] CheckerRequest request)
    {
        try
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Received validation request: {Intent}", request.Intent);

            // Get the named gRPC client for Checker service
            var httpClientFactory = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>();
            var httpClient = httpClientFactory.CreateClient("GrpcClient_checker");
            
            var isHttps = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("DOTNET_LAUNCHPROFILE") == "https";
            var channel = Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannel.ForAddress(
                $"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://checker-agent",
                new Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannelOptions { HttpClient = httpClient });
            var checkerClient = new AgentService.AgentServiceClient(channel);

            // Call the gRPC service
            var grpcRequest = new AgentRequest
            {
                Intent = request.Intent,
                ContextJson = request.ContextJson ?? string.Empty
            };

            var callOptions = new CallOptions(deadline: DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(5));
            var grpcResponse = await checkerClient.ExecuteTaskAsync(grpcRequest, callOptions);

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Validation completed successfully");

            return Ok(new CheckerResponse
            {
                Content = grpcResponse.Content,
                Success = grpcResponse.Success
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Validation request failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new CheckerResponse
            {
                Content = $"Error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            });
        }
    }
}

public class CheckerRequest
{
    public string Intent { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string? ContextJson { get; set; }
}

public class CheckerResponse
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public bool Success { get; set; }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.OrchestrationApi\Controllers\MakerController.cs

using System;
using Grpc.Core;
using Grpc.Net.Client;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API controller for the Maker Agent Service
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Produces("application/json")]
public class MakerController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ILogger<MakerController> _logger;
    private readonly IServiceProvider _serviceProvider;

    public MakerController(
        ILogger<MakerController> logger,
        IServiceProvider serviceProvider)
    {
        _logger = logger;
        _serviceProvider = serviceProvider;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Execute an implementation task via the Maker gRPC service
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="request">The implementation request with plan/intent</param>
    /// <returns>The maker's response</returns>
    [HttpPost("make")]
    [ProducesResponseType(typeof(MakerResponse), StatusCodes.Status200OK)]
    [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]
    public async Task<IActionResult> Make([FromBody] MakerRequest request)
    {
        try
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("üî® Received implementation request: {Intent}", request.Intent);

            // Get the named gRPC client for Maker service
            // AddGrpcClient registers a factory, access it via the HttpClient name pattern
            // The factory is registered with name "maker", access via IHttpClientFactory
            var httpClientFactory = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>();
            var httpClient = httpClientFactory.CreateClient("GrpcClient_maker");
            
            // Create gRPC channel and client
            var isHttps = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("DOTNET_LAUNCHPROFILE") == "https";
            var channel = Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannel.ForAddress(
                $"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://maker-agent",
                new Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannelOptions { HttpClient = httpClient });
            var makerClient = new AgentService.AgentServiceClient(channel);

            // Call the gRPC service using injected client
            var grpcRequest = new AgentRequest
            {
                Intent = request.Intent,
                ContextJson = request.ContextJson ?? string.Empty
            };

            // Set deadline for gRPC call to accommodate long-running Ollama inference
            // Maker makes multiple Ollama calls (tool loading + execution), can take 1-3 minutes
            // Allow up to 10 minutes to match TotalRequestTimeout configuration
            var callOptions = new CallOptions(deadline: DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(10));
            var grpcResponse = await makerClient.ExecuteTaskAsync(grpcRequest, callOptions);

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Implementation completed successfully");

            return Ok(new MakerResponse
            {
                Content = grpcResponse.Content,
                Success = grpcResponse.Success
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Implementation request failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new MakerResponse
            {
                Content = $"Error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            });
        }
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Request model for making/implementation
/// </summary>
public class MakerRequest
{
    /// <summary>
    /// The plan or intent to implement
    /// </summary>
    public string Intent { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    /// <summary>
    /// Optional context in JSON format (e.g., plan from Planner)
    /// </summary>
    public string? ContextJson { get; set; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Response model from maker
/// </summary>
public class MakerResponse
{
    /// <summary>
    /// The maker's response content (code, artifacts, etc.)
    /// </summary>
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    /// <summary>
    /// Whether the implementation was successful
    /// </summary>
    public bool Success { get; set; }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using System.Net.Http;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// Simple test controller to directly call Ollama - bypasses gRPC to isolate issues
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Produces("application/json")]
public class OllamaTestController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ILogger<OllamaTestController> _logger;
    private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
    private readonly IConfiguration _configuration;

    public OllamaTestController(
        ILogger<OllamaTestController> logger,
        IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory,
        IConfiguration configuration)
    {
        _logger = logger;
        _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        _configuration = configuration;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Test direct Ollama API call - simple test to verify Ollama works
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost("test")]
    [ProducesResponseType(typeof(OllamaTestResponse), StatusCodes.Status200OK)]
    [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]
    public async Task<IActionResult> TestOllama([FromBody] OllamaTestRequest request)
    {
        try
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("üß™ Testing direct Ollama connection...");

            // Get Ollama URI from configuration (same as PlannerService uses)
            var ollamaConnectionString = _configuration.GetConnectionString("ollama");
            
            _logger.LogInformation("üîç Ollama connection string from config: {ConnectionString}", ollamaConnectionString ?? "NULL");

            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(ollamaConnectionString))
            {
                return StatusCode(500, new OllamaTestResponse
                {
                    Success = false,
                    Message = "Ollama connection string not found in configuration. Ensure the service references ollama in AppHost.",
                    Error = "Configuration missing 'ConnectionStrings:ollama'"
                });
            }

            // Parse connection string - could be "Endpoint=http://..." or just a URI
            Uri uri;
            if (ollamaConnectionString.StartsWith("Endpoint=", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                // Extract URI from "Endpoint=http://..." format
                var endpointValue = ollamaConnectionString.Substring("Endpoint=".Length).Trim();
                Uri? parsedUri;
                if (!Uri.TryCreate(endpointValue, UriKind.Absolute, out parsedUri))
                {
                    return StatusCode(500, new OllamaTestResponse
                    {
                        Success = false,
                        Message = $"Invalid Ollama endpoint in connection string: {endpointValue}",
                        Error = "Cannot parse endpoint URI"
                    });
                }
                uri = parsedUri;
            }
            else
            {
                // Assume it's a direct URI
                Uri? parsedUri;
                if (!Uri.TryCreate(ollamaConnectionString, UriKind.Absolute, out parsedUri))
                {
                    return StatusCode(500, new OllamaTestResponse
                    {
                        Success = false,
                        Message = $"Invalid Ollama URI: {ollamaConnectionString}",
                        Error = "Cannot parse URI"
                    });
                }
                uri = parsedUri;
            }

            _logger.LogInformation("üì° Connecting to Ollama at: {Uri}", uri);

            // Use the named client configured with long timeout and custom resilience handler
            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ollama-direct");
            httpClient.BaseAddress = uri;

            // Prepare Ollama API request
            var ollamaRequest = new
            {
                model = "qwen2.5:7b",
                messages = new[]
                {
                    new { role = "user", content = request.Prompt ?? "Say hello in one sentence." }
                },
                stream = false
            };

            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(ollamaRequest);
            var content = new StringContent(json, Encoding.UTF8, "application/json");

            _logger.LogInformation("üì§ Sending request to Ollama...");

            // Make the request
            var startTime = DateTime.UtcNow;
            var response = await httpClient.PostAsync("/api/chat", content);
            var elapsed = DateTime.UtcNow - startTime;

            _logger.LogInformation("‚è±Ô∏è Ollama responded in {Elapsed}ms", elapsed.TotalMilliseconds);

            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var responseContent = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Ollama response received: {Length} bytes", responseContent.Length);

                return Ok(new OllamaTestResponse
                {
                    Success = true,
                    Message = "Ollama connection successful!",
                    ResponseTimeMs = elapsed.TotalMilliseconds,
                    Response = responseContent
                });
            }
            else
            {
                var errorContent = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                _logger.LogError("‚ùå Ollama returned error: {StatusCode} - {Error}", response.StatusCode, errorContent);

                return StatusCode(500, new OllamaTestResponse
                {
                    Success = false,
                    Message = $"Ollama error: {response.StatusCode}",
                    ResponseTimeMs = elapsed.TotalMilliseconds,
                    Error = errorContent
                });
            }
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Ollama test failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new OllamaTestResponse
            {
                Success = false,
                Message = $"Error: {ex.Message}",
                Error = ex.ToString()
            });
        }
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Request model for Ollama test
/// </summary>
public class OllamaTestRequest
{
    /// <summary>
    /// The prompt to send to Ollama
    /// </summary>
    public string? Prompt { get; set; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Response model from Ollama test
/// </summary>
public class OllamaTestResponse
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Whether the test was successful
    /// </summary>
    public bool Success { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// Status message
    /// </summary>
    public string Message { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    /// <summary>
    /// Response time in milliseconds
    /// </summary>
    public double ResponseTimeMs { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// Raw response from Ollama (if successful)
    /// </summary>
    public string? Response { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// Error details (if failed)
    /// </summary>
    public string? Error { get; set; }
}

using System;
using Grpc.Core;
using Grpc.Net.Client;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API controller for the Orchestrator Agent Service
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Produces("application/json")]
public class OrchestratorController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ILogger<OrchestratorController> _logger;
    private readonly IServiceProvider _serviceProvider;

    public OrchestratorController(
        ILogger<OrchestratorController> logger,
        IServiceProvider serviceProvider)
    {
        _logger = logger;
        _serviceProvider = serviceProvider;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Execute an orchestration task via the Orchestrator gRPC service
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="request">The orchestration request with high-level goal</param>
    /// <returns>The orchestrator's response</returns>
    [HttpPost("orchestrate")]
    [ProducesResponseType(typeof(OrchestratorResponse), StatusCodes.Status200OK)]
    [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]
    public async Task<IActionResult> Orchestrate([FromBody] OrchestratorRequest request)
    {
        try
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("üéØ Received orchestration request: {Intent}", request.Intent);

            // Get the named gRPC client for Orchestrator service
            var httpClientFactory = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>();
            var httpClient = httpClientFactory.CreateClient("GrpcClient_orchestrator");
            
            var isHttps = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("DOTNET_LAUNCHPROFILE") == "https";
            var channel = Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannel.ForAddress(
                $"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://orchestrator-agent",
                new Grpc.Net.Client.GrpcChannelOptions { HttpClient = httpClient });
            var orchestratorClient = new AgentService.AgentServiceClient(channel);

            // Call the gRPC service
            var grpcRequest = new AgentRequest
            {
                Intent = request.Intent,
                ContextJson = request.ContextJson ?? string.Empty
            };

            var callOptions = new CallOptions(deadline: DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(5));
            var grpcResponse = await orchestratorClient.ExecuteTaskAsync(grpcRequest, callOptions);

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Orchestration completed successfully");

            return Ok(new OrchestratorResponse
            {
                Content = grpcResponse.Content,
                Success = grpcResponse.Success
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Orchestration request failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new OrchestratorResponse
            {
                Content = $"Error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            });
        }
    }
}

public class OrchestratorRequest
{
    public string Intent { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string? ContextJson { get; set; }
}

public class OrchestratorResponse
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public bool Success { get; set; }
}

using System;
using Grpc.Core;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using ProjectName.Shared.Grpc;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API controller for the Planner Agent Service
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Produces("application/json")]
public class PlannerController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ILogger<PlannerController> _logger;
    private readonly AgentService.AgentServiceClient _plannerClient;

    public PlannerController(
        ILogger<PlannerController> logger,
        AgentService.AgentServiceClient plannerClient)
    {
        _logger = logger;
        _plannerClient = plannerClient;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Execute a planning task via the Planner gRPC service
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="request">The planning request with intent</param>
    /// <returns>The planner's response</returns>
    [HttpPost("plan")]
    [ProducesResponseType(typeof(PlannerResponse), StatusCodes.Status200OK)]
    [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]
    public async Task<IActionResult> Plan([FromBody] PlannerRequest request)
    {
        try
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("üìã Received planning request: {Intent}", request.Intent);

            // Call the gRPC service using injected client
            var grpcRequest = new AgentRequest
            {
                Intent = request.Intent,
                ContextJson = request.ContextJson ?? string.Empty
            };

            // Set deadline for gRPC call to accommodate long-running Ollama inference
            // Default is 30s which is too short - allow up to 5 minutes
            var callOptions = new CallOptions(deadline: DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(5));
            var grpcResponse = await _plannerClient.ExecuteTaskAsync(grpcRequest, callOptions);

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Planning completed successfully");

            return Ok(new PlannerResponse
            {
                Content = grpcResponse.Content,
                Success = grpcResponse.Success
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Planning request failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new PlannerResponse
            {
                Content = $"Error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            });
        }
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.OrchestrationApi\Controllers\WorkflowController.cs
================================================================================

using System.Text.Json;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;
using ProjectName.Workflow.Services;
using ProjectName.Workflow.Workflows;

namespace ProjectName.OrchestrationApi.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// REST API controller for PMCR-O Workflow execution
/// Uses Microsoft Agents AI Workflows for orchestration
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
public class WorkflowController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly IChatClient _chatClient;
    private readonly AgentMcpToolsHelper _mcpToolsHelper;
    private readonly ILoggerFactory _loggerFactory;
    private readonly LanguageDetector _languageDetector;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;
    private readonly ILogger<WorkflowController> _logger;

    public WorkflowController(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        LanguageDetector languageDetector,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext,
        ILogger<WorkflowController> logger)
    {
        _chatClient = chatClient;
        _mcpToolsHelper = mcpToolsHelper;
        _loggerFactory = loggerFactory;
        _languageDetector = languageDetector;
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
        _logger = logger;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Execute PMCR-O workflow with automatic language detection
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost("execute")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<WorkflowResponse>> ExecuteWorkflow([FromBody] WorkflowRequest request)
    {
        _logger.LogInformation("üîÑ Starting PMCR-O workflow for intent: {Intent}", request.Intent);

        try
        {
            // Detect language from intent
            var language = _languageDetector.DetectLanguage(request.Intent);
            _logger.LogInformation("üåê Detected language: {Language}", language);

            // Clear shared context for new workflow execution
            _sharedContext.Clear();
            
            // Create workflow with shared context
            var workflowFactory = new PmcroWorkflow(_chatClient, _mcpToolsHelper, _loggerFactory, _sharedContext);
            var workflow = workflowFactory.CreateWorkflow();

            // Execute workflow
            // Note: Workflows need a TurnToken to trigger execution
            await using var run = await InProcessExecution.StreamAsync(workflow, request.Intent);
            
            // Send TurnToken to trigger workflow execution
            await run.TrySendMessageAsync(new TurnToken(emitEvents: true));

            // Collect output
            var output = new System.Text.StringBuilder();
            await foreach (var evt in run.WatchStreamAsync())
            {
                if (evt is WorkflowOutputEvent outputEvent)
                {
                    if (outputEvent.Data != null)
                    {
                        // Check if Data is a string
                        if (outputEvent.Data is string str)
                        {
                            output.AppendLine(str);
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            // Serialize object to JSON for proper output
                            try
                            {
                                var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(outputEvent.Data, new JsonSerializerOptions
                                {
                                    WriteIndented = true,
                                    PropertyNamingPolicy = JsonNamingPolicy.CamelCase
                                });
                                output.AppendLine(json);
                            }
                            catch (Exception ex)
                            {
                                // Fallback to ToString if serialization fails
                                output.AppendLine($"Output: {outputEvent.Data}");
                                _logger.LogWarning(ex, "Failed to serialize workflow output event data");
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                else if (evt is AgentRunUpdateEvent agentUpdate)
                {
                    // Also capture agent updates
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(agentUpdate.Update?.Text))
                    {
                        output.AppendLine(agentUpdate.Update.Text);
                    }
                }
            }

            _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ PMCR-O workflow completed");

            return Ok(new WorkflowResponse
            {
                Content = output.ToString(),
                Success = true,
                Language = language.ToString()
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå PMCR-O workflow failed");
            return StatusCode(500, new WorkflowResponse
            {
                Content = $"Workflow error: {ex.Message}",
                Success = false
            });
        }
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Get the shared context activity summary (Round Table Logs)
    /// Shows the conversation history between agents
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("context")]
    public ActionResult<ContextResponse> GetContext()
    {
        try
        {
            var summary = _sharedContext.GetActivitySummary(count: 50);
            var recentThoughts = _sharedContext.GetRecentThoughts(count: 50);
            
            return Ok(new ContextResponse
            {
                ActivitySummary = summary,
                RecentThoughts = recentThoughts.Select(t => new ThoughtDto
                {
                    AgentName = t.AgentName,
                    ThoughtType = t.ThoughtType.ToString(),
                    Content = t.Content,
                    Timestamp = t.Timestamp,
                    Metadata = t.Metadata
                }).ToList()
            });
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            _logger.LogError(ex, "‚ùå Failed to get shared context");
            return StatusCode(500, new ContextResponse
            {
                ActivitySummary = $"Error retrieving context: {ex.Message}",
                RecentThoughts = new List<ThoughtDto>()
            });
        }
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Request model for workflow execution
/// </summary>
public class WorkflowRequest
{
    public string Intent { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string? ContextJson { get; set; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Response model for workflow execution
/// </summary>
public class WorkflowResponse
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public bool Success { get; set; }
    public string? Language { get; set; }
}

/// <summary>
/// Response model for shared context
/// </summary>
public class ContextResponse
{
    public string ActivitySummary { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public List<ThoughtDto> RecentThoughts { get; set; } = new();
}

/// <summary>
/// DTO for agent thoughts
/// </summary>
public class ThoughtDto
{
    public string AgentName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string ThoughtType { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public DateTime Timestamp { get; set; }
    public Dictionary<string, string> Metadata { get; set; } = new();
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.OrchestrationApi\Program.cs
================================================================================

using System.Net.Http;
using System.Net.Sockets;
using System.Threading;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Http.Resilience;
using OllamaSharp;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.AddServiceDefaults();

// Add services to the container
builder.Services.AddControllers();
builder.Services.AddEndpointsApiExplorer();

// Register workflow services
builder.Services.AddSingleton<ProjectName.Shared.Services.AgentMcpToolsHelper>();
builder.Services.AddSingleton<ProjectName.Workflow.Services.LanguageDetector>();
builder.Services.AddSingleton<ProjectName.Shared.Services.SharedContextManager>(); // Shared context for agent collaboration

// Register IChatClient for workflows (using Ollama)
var ollamaConnectionString = builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("ollama");
if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(ollamaConnectionString))
{
    // Parse connection string - could be "Endpoint=http://..." or just a URI
    Uri uri;
    if (ollamaConnectionString.StartsWith("Endpoint=", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
    {
        // Extract URI from "Endpoint=http://..." format
        var endpointValue = ollamaConnectionString.Substring("Endpoint=".Length).Trim();
        if (!Uri.TryCreate(endpointValue, UriKind.Absolute, out var parsedUri))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"Invalid Ollama endpoint in connection string: {endpointValue}");
        }
        uri = parsedUri;
    }
    else
    {
        // Try to parse as direct URI
        if (!Uri.TryCreate(ollamaConnectionString, UriKind.Absolute, out var directUri))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"Invalid Ollama connection string format: {ollamaConnectionString}");
        }
        uri = directUri;
    }
    
    var modelId = "qwen2.5-coder:7b";
    
    builder.Services.AddHttpClient("ollama-workflow", client =>
    {
        client.BaseAddress = uri;
        client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
    })
    .ConfigurePrimaryHttpMessageHandler(() => new System.Net.Http.SocketsHttpHandler
    {
        ConnectTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30),
        PooledConnectionLifetime = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10),
        PooledConnectionIdleTimeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)
    })
    // Remove default resilience handler first, then add custom one for long-running workflow operations
    // Workflows can take 5-10 minutes with multiple agent calls
    .RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
    .AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
    {
        // Increase attempt timeout to accommodate Ollama inference (can take 30s-2min on CPU)
        // Workflows make multiple agent calls, so need longer timeout
        options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
        
        // Total request timeout (all retries combined) - must be longer than attempt timeout
        // Workflows can take 5-10 minutes total with multiple agent calls
        options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10);
        
        // Reduce retry attempts for long-running operations
        options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 1; // Don't retry long operations
        
        // Circuit breaker sampling duration must be at least double the attempt timeout
        options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(12);
    });

    // ‚úÖ CRITICAL FIX: Register IChatClient with UseFunctionInvocation middleware for workflows
    builder.Services.AddSingleton<Microsoft.Extensions.AI.IChatClient>(sp =>
    {
        var httpClient = sp.GetRequiredService<IHttpClientFactory>().CreateClient("ollama-workflow");
        var baseClient = new OllamaApiClient(httpClient, modelId);
        
        return new ChatClientBuilder(baseClient)
            .UseFunctionInvocation() // ‚úÖ Critical middleware
            .Build();
    });
}

// Configure HttpClient for direct Ollama calls (bypasses gRPC for testing)
builder.Services.AddHttpClient("ollama-direct", client =>
{
    client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
})
.ConfigurePrimaryHttpMessageHandler(() => new System.Net.Http.SocketsHttpHandler
{
    ConnectTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30),
    PooledConnectionLifetime = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10),
    PooledConnectionIdleTimeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5)
})
// Remove default resilience handler and add custom one for long-running LLM calls
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// Register gRPC clients for agent services using Aspire service discovery
// The service names will be resolved automatically by Aspire
var isHttps = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("DOTNET_LAUNCHPROFILE") == "https";

// Planner Service gRPC client (default/named)
builder.Services.AddGrpcClient<ProjectName.Shared.Grpc.AgentService.AgentServiceClient>(options =>
{
    // Use HTTP for local development (Aspire default)
    // Service discovery will resolve "planner-agent" to actual endpoint
    options.Address = new Uri($"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://planner-agent");
})
.AddServiceDiscovery() // CRITICAL: Enables Aspire service discovery for gRPC
.ConfigureHttpClient(client =>
{
    // Set HttpClient timeout to infinite - let resilience handler control it
    client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
})
// Remove default resilience handler first, then add custom one
// The default from AddServiceDefaults() has 30s timeout which is too short
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    // Increase attempt timeout to accommodate Ollama inference (can take 30s-2min on CPU)
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    
    // Total request timeout (all retries combined)
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    
    // Reduce retry attempts for long-running operations
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    
    // Circuit breaker sampling duration must be at least double the attempt timeout
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// Maker Service gRPC client (keyed)
builder.Services.AddGrpcClient<ProjectName.Shared.Grpc.AgentService.AgentServiceClient>("maker", options =>
{
    // Use HTTP for local development (Aspire default)
    // Service discovery will resolve "maker-agent" to actual endpoint
    options.Address = new Uri($"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://maker-agent");
})
.AddServiceDiscovery() // CRITICAL: Enables Aspire service discovery for gRPC
.ConfigureHttpClient(client =>
{
    // Set HttpClient timeout to infinite - let resilience handler control it
    client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan;
})
// Remove default resilience handler first, then add custom one
// IMPORTANT: Must remove BEFORE adding new handler, and configure BEFORE AddServiceDiscovery if needed
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    // Increase attempt timeout to accommodate Ollama inference (can take 30s-2min on CPU)
    // Maker may make multiple Ollama calls (tool loading + execution), so need longer timeout
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    
    // Total request timeout (all retries combined) - must be longer than attempt timeout
    // Maker can take 1-3 minutes total with multiple Ollama calls
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10);
    
    // Reduce retry attempts for long-running operations
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 1; // Don't retry long operations
    
    // Circuit breaker sampling duration must be at least double the attempt timeout
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(12);
});

// Checker Service gRPC client
builder.Services.AddGrpcClient<ProjectName.Shared.Grpc.AgentService.AgentServiceClient>("checker", options =>
{
    options.Address = new Uri($"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://checker-agent");
})
.AddServiceDiscovery()
.ConfigureHttpClient(client => client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan)
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// Reflector Service gRPC client
builder.Services.AddGrpcClient<ProjectName.Shared.Grpc.AgentService.AgentServiceClient>("reflector", options =>
{
    options.Address = new Uri($"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://reflector-agent");
})
.AddServiceDiscovery()
.ConfigureHttpClient(client => client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan)
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// Orchestrator Service gRPC client
builder.Services.AddGrpcClient<ProjectName.Shared.Grpc.AgentService.AgentServiceClient>("orchestrator", options =>
{
    options.Address = new Uri($"{(isHttps ? "https" : "http")}://orchestrator-agent");
})
.AddServiceDiscovery()
.ConfigureHttpClient(client => client.Timeout = Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan)
.RemoveAllResilienceHandlers()
.AddStandardResilienceHandler(options =>
{
    options.AttemptTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(3);
    options.TotalRequestTimeout.Timeout = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
    options.Retry.MaxRetryAttempts = 2;
    options.CircuitBreaker.SamplingDuration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(6);
});

// Configure Swagger/OpenAPI
builder.Services.AddSwaggerGen(c =>
{
    c.SwaggerDoc("v1", new Microsoft.OpenApi.Models.OpenApiInfo
    {
        Title = "PMCR-O Orchestration API",
        Version = "v1",
        Description = "REST API gateway for PMCR-O agent services. This API provides HTTP endpoints that communicate with gRPC-based agent services.",
        Contact = new Microsoft.OpenApi.Models.OpenApiContact
        {
            Name = "PMCR-O System",
            Email = "pmcro@example.com"
        }
    });

    // Include XML comments if available
    var xmlFile = $"{System.Reflection.Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetName().Name}.xml";
    var xmlPath = Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, xmlFile);
    if (File.Exists(xmlPath))
    {
        c.IncludeXmlComments(xmlPath);
    }
});

var app = builder.Build();

app.MapDefaultEndpoints();

// Configure the HTTP request pipeline
if (app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseSwagger();
    app.UseSwaggerUI(c =>
    {
        c.SwaggerEndpoint("/swagger/v1/swagger.json", "PMCR-O Orchestration API v1");
        c.RoutePrefix = string.Empty; // Set Swagger UI at the app's root
    });
}

app.UseHttpsRedirection();
app.UseAuthorization();
app.MapControllers();

app.Run();
