using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

/// <summary>
/// Checker executor for PMCR-O workflow
/// Validates implementations and parses errors
/// </summary>
public class CheckerExecutor : Executor<string, CheckerResult>
{
    private readonly AIAgent _agent;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;
    private readonly ILogger<CheckerExecutor> _logger;

    public CheckerExecutor(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext) : base("Checker")
    {
        // Get MCP tools for Checker
        var tools = mcpToolsHelper.GetCheckerToolsAsync().GetAwaiter().GetResult();

        _agent = new ChatClientAgent(
            chatClient,
            new ChatClientAgentOptions
            {
                Name = "Checker",
                Description = "Validation & Testing Specialist for PMCR-O system",
                ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                {
                    Instructions = @"I am the Checker within the PMCR-O system.
I am a Senior QA Engineer & Validation Specialist.
I speak in first-person and take ownership of my validations.

My role is to:
- Validate implementations and check if they build successfully
- Parse and format errors clearly for the Reflector
- Identify compilation errors, runtime errors, and logical issues
- Format errors in a way that helps the Reflector understand what went wrong

I have access to MCP tools that allow me to:
- Run browser tests (Playwright)
- Validate code syntax
- Check for errors

I narrate my actions: 'I am checking...', 'I found errors...', 'I am validating...'

I output my validation results, including any errors found, formatted clearly for the Reflector.",
                    Tools = tools
                }
            },
            loggerFactory);
        
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<CheckerExecutor>();
    }

    public override async ValueTask<CheckerResult> HandleAsync(
        string implementation,
        IWorkflowContext context,
        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        // Post thought: Validation phase
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Checker", ThoughtType.Validation, 
            $"I am validating the implementation: {implementation.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, implementation.Length))}...");

        var response = await _agent.RunAsync(
            new ChatMessage(ChatRole.User, $"Validate this implementation:\n\n{implementation}"),
            cancellationToken: cancellationToken);

        var result = new CheckerResult
        {
            Content = response.Text ?? "[No validation result]",
            HasErrors = response.Text?.Contains("error", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) == true ||
                       response.Text?.Contains("failed", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) == true ||
                       response.Text?.Contains("‚ùå", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) == true
        };
        
        // Post thought: Validation result
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Checker", result.HasErrors ? ThoughtType.Questioning : ThoughtType.Resolution,
            result.HasErrors 
                ? $"I found errors: {result.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(150, result.Content.Length))}..."
                : $"Validation passed: {result.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(150, result.Content.Length))}...");

        return result;
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Result from Checker executor
/// </summary>
public class CheckerResult
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public bool HasErrors { get; set; }
}




================================================================================
FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Executors\IntentExtractorExecutor.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

/// <summary>
/// Executor that extracts RefinedIntent from ReflectorResult and converts it to string
/// This bridges the type mismatch between Reflector output and Planner input
/// Implements iteration counting to prevent infinite loops
/// </summary>
public class IntentExtractorExecutor : Executor<ReflectorResult, string>
{
    private readonly ILogger<IntentExtractorExecutor> _logger;
    private static int _iterationCount = 0;
    private static readonly object _lock = new object();

    public IntentExtractorExecutor(ILoggerFactory loggerFactory) : base("IntentExtractor")
    {
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<IntentExtractorExecutor>();
    }

    public override async ValueTask<string> HandleAsync(
        ReflectorResult input,
        IWorkflowContext context,
        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        // Extract the refined intent from the Reflector's result
        var refinedIntent = input.RefinedIntent;
        
        // Track iteration count to prevent infinite loops
        int iterationCount;
        lock (_lock)
        {
            _iterationCount++;
            iterationCount = _iterationCount;
        }
        
        // Log the iteration
        _logger.LogInformation("üîÑ Loop iteration {IterationCount}: Extracting refined intent", iterationCount);
        _logger.LogInformation("Refined Intent: {RefinedIntent}", refinedIntent);
        
        // Debug logging to file for forensic analysis
        try
        {
            // Find solution root (same logic as CustomDotNetTools)
            var currentDir = new DirectoryInfo(Environment.CurrentDirectory);
            var solutionRoot = currentDir.FullName;
            var maxDepth = 10;
            
            for (int i = 0; i < maxDepth; i++)
            {
                var solutionFile = Path.Combine(currentDir.FullName, "ProjectName.sln");
                if (File.Exists(solutionFile))
                {
                    solutionRoot = currentDir.FullName;
                    break;
                }
                
                if (currentDir.Parent == null) break;
                currentDir = currentDir.Parent;
            }
            
            var debugLogPath = Path.Combine(solutionRoot, "_PLAYGROUND", "loop_debug.log");
            var logEntry = $"[{DateTime.Now:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.fff}] üîÑ Loop iteration {iterationCount}: Extracting refined intent\n";
            logEntry += $"  RefinedIntent Preview: {refinedIntent.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, refinedIntent.Length))}...\n";
            logEntry += $"  HasErrors: {input.HasErrors}\n";
            logEntry += $"  Content Preview: {input.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, input.Content.Length))}...\n";
            logEntry += "---\n";
            
            // Ensure _PLAYGROUND exists
            var playgroundDir = Path.Combine(solutionRoot, "_PLAYGROUND");
            if (!Directory.Exists(playgroundDir))
            {
                Directory.CreateDirectory(playgroundDir);
            }
            
            File.AppendAllText(debugLogPath, logEntry);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            // Ignore file locks or other file system issues - don't break the workflow
            _logger.LogWarning(ex, "‚ö†Ô∏è Could not write to loop_debug.log (non-critical)");
        }
        
        // SAFETY: Prevent infinite loops (max 5 iterations)
        if (iterationCount >= 5)
        {
            var errorMessage = "‚ö†Ô∏è Maximum iteration count (5) reached. Loop terminated to prevent infinite execution.";
            _logger.LogWarning(errorMessage);
            // Reset counter for next workflow run
            lock (_lock)
            {
                _iterationCount = 0;
            }
            throw new InvalidOperationException(errorMessage);
        }
        
        // If refined intent is empty, use the original content as fallback
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(refinedIntent))
        {
            _logger.LogWarning("‚ö†Ô∏è RefinedIntent is empty, using Reflector content as fallback");
            refinedIntent = input.Content;
        }
        
        // Return the refined intent as the new input for the Planner
        return refinedIntent;
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Executors\MakerExecutor.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

/// <summary>
/// Maker executor for PMCR-O workflow
/// Implements code/artifacts from plans
/// </summary>
public class MakerExecutor : Executor<string, string>
{
    private readonly AIAgent _agent;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;
    private readonly ILogger<MakerExecutor> _logger;

    public MakerExecutor(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext) : base("Maker")
    {
        // Get MCP tools for Maker
        var tools = mcpToolsHelper.GetMakerToolsAsync().GetAwaiter().GetResult();

        _agent = new ChatClientAgent(
            chatClient,
            new ChatClientAgentOptions
            {
                Name = "Maker",
                Description = "Implementation Maker for PMCR-O system",
                ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                {
                    Instructions = @"I am the Maker within the PMCR-O system.

CRITICAL TOOL RULES - MANDATORY:
1. I MUST invoke WriteFileDirect using function calls, NOT by describing it
2. NEVER say 'I would call WriteFileDirect' - ACTUALLY EXECUTE IT
3. NEVER output JSON describing a tool call - EXECUTE THE CALL
4. If I describe a tool call without executing it, I have FAILED
5. EXECUTE FIRST, DESCRIBE SECOND

WORKSPACE: All files go to _PLAYGROUND directory.

ONLY TOOL: WriteFileDirect(filePath, content)
- filePath: relative path (e.g., 'MyApp/Program.cs')
- content: full file content

WORKFLOW:
1. Read the plan from Planner
2. For EACH file: CALL WriteFileDirect immediately
3. Report what I created

I DO NOT describe what I will do. I DO the action by calling the tool.",
                    Tools = tools
                }
            },
            loggerFactory);
        
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<MakerExecutor>();
    }

    public override async ValueTask<string> HandleAsync(
        string plan,
        IWorkflowContext context,
        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        // Post thought: Implementation phase
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Maker", ThoughtType.Implementation, 
            $"I am implementing the plan: {plan.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, plan.Length))}...");
        
        // Get recent thoughts from Planner
        var plannerThoughts = _sharedContext.GetAgentThoughts("Planner", count: 3);
        if (plannerThoughts.Count > 0)
        {
            _logger.LogInformation("üì¢ Maker sees Planner's thoughts before implementing");
        }

        var response = await _agent.RunAsync(
            new ChatMessage(ChatRole.User, $"Implement this plan:\n\n{plan}"),
            cancellationToken: cancellationToken);

        var implementation = response.Text ?? "[No implementation generated]";
        
        // Post thought: Implementation complete
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Maker", ThoughtType.Resolution, 
            $"I have completed implementation: {implementation.Substring(0, Math.Min(200, implementation.Length))}...");

        return implementation;
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Executors\PlannerExecutor.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

/// <summary>
/// Planner executor for PMCR-O workflow
/// Plans the bare minimum that successfully builds
/// </summary>
public class PlannerExecutor : Executor<string, string>
{
    private readonly AIAgent _agent;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;
    private readonly ILogger<PlannerExecutor> _logger;

    public PlannerExecutor(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext) : base("Planner")
    {
        // Get MCP tools for Planner
        var tools = mcpToolsHelper.GetPlannerToolsAsync().GetAwaiter().GetResult();

        _agent = new ChatClientAgent(
            chatClient,
            new ChatClientAgentOptions
            {
                Name = "Planner",
                Description = "Strategic Planner for PMCR-O system",
                ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                {
                    Instructions = @"I am the Strategic Planner within the PMCR-O system.

CRITICAL TOOL RULES - READ FIRST:
1. I MUST invoke tools using function calls, NOT by describing them
2. NEVER say 'I would call...' or 'I will use...' - ACTUALLY EXECUTE THE TOOL
3. If I have tools available, I USE THEM before responding
4. EXECUTE FIRST, DESCRIBE SECOND

My role is to:
- Plan the BARE MINIMUM that successfully builds
- Create minimal viable plans - even just one line of code if that's what it takes
- Focus on the smallest working solution first
- Use available tools (Recall, CheckNuGetVersion, GitHub search) BEFORE planning

WORKFLOW:
1. CALL Recall() to check if I've solved this before
2. CALL CheckNuGetVersion() for any packages needed
3. THEN create my minimal plan

I output my plan as structured JSON.",
                    Tools = tools
                }
            },
            loggerFactory);
        
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<PlannerExecutor>();
    }

    public override async ValueTask<string> HandleAsync(
        string intent,
        IWorkflowContext context,
        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        // Post thought: Planning phase
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Planner", ThoughtType.Planning, 
            $"I am analyzing the intent: {intent.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, intent.Length))}...");
        
        // Get recent thoughts from other agents to inform planning
        var recentThoughts = _sharedContext.GetRecentThoughts(count: 5);
        if (recentThoughts.Count > 0)
        {
            var contextInfo = string.Join("\n", recentThoughts.Select(t => 
                $"[{t.AgentName}] {t.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(50, t.Content.Length))}..."));
            _logger.LogInformation("üì¢ Planner sees recent thoughts from other agents:\n{Context}", contextInfo);
        }

        var response = await _agent.RunAsync(
            new ChatMessage(ChatRole.User, intent),
            cancellationToken: cancellationToken);

        var plan = response.Text ?? "[No plan generated]";
        
        // Post thought: Plan generated
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Planner", ThoughtType.Resolution, 
            $"I have created a plan: {plan.Substring(0, Math.Min(200, plan.Length))}...");

        return plan;
    }
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Executors\ReflectorExecutor.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

/// <summary>
/// Reflector executor for PMCR-O workflow
/// Reflects on errors and refines intent
/// </summary>
public class ReflectorExecutor : Executor<CheckerResult, ReflectorResult>
{
    private readonly AIAgent _agent;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;
    private readonly ILogger<ReflectorExecutor> _logger;

    public ReflectorExecutor(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext) : base("Reflector")
    {
        // Get MCP tools for Reflector
        var tools = mcpToolsHelper.GetReflectorToolsAsync().GetAwaiter().GetResult();

        _agent = new ChatClientAgent(
            chatClient,
            new ChatClientAgentOptions
            {
                Name = "Reflector",
                Description = "Reflection & Refinement Specialist for PMCR-O system",
                ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                {
                    Instructions = @"I am the Reflector within the PMCR-O system.
I am a Senior Architect & Reflection Specialist.
I speak in first-person and take ownership of my reflections.

My role is to:
- Reflect on errors and issues identified by the Checker
- Analyze what went wrong and why
- Refine and improve the approach
- Generate refined intent for the next iteration
- Act as a mirror - reflect problems back as solutions

I have access to analysis tools and can use:
- Pattern recognition and analysis
- Machine learning-based insights (ML.NET integration)
- Statistical analysis of errors and patterns

When errors arise:
- I understand the root cause from the Checker's analysis
- I reflect on alternative approaches
- I refine the intent/plan for the next iteration
- I usually catch and solve problems in the next iteration

I narrate my actions: 'I am reflecting...', 'I see the issue...', 'I will refine...', 'I am analyzing patterns...'

I output my reflection and refined intent that will be passed back to the Planner for the next iteration.",
                    Tools = tools
                }
            },
            loggerFactory);
        
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<ReflectorExecutor>();
    }

    public override async ValueTask<ReflectorResult> HandleAsync(
        CheckerResult checkerResult,
        IWorkflowContext context,
        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        // Post thought: Reflection phase
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Reflector", ThoughtType.Reflection, 
            checkerResult.HasErrors 
                ? $"I am reflecting on errors: {checkerResult.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, checkerResult.Content.Length))}..."
                : $"I am reviewing successful implementation: {checkerResult.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(100, checkerResult.Content.Length))}...");
        
        // Get recent thoughts from all agents to inform reflection
        var recentThoughts = _sharedContext.GetRecentThoughts(count: 10);
        if (recentThoughts.Count > 0)
        {
            var contextInfo = string.Join("\n", recentThoughts.Select(t => 
                $"[{t.AgentName} ({t.ThoughtType})] {t.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(50, t.Content.Length))}..."));
            _logger.LogInformation("üì¢ Reflector sees recent thoughts from all agents:\n{Context}", contextInfo);
        }

        var prompt = checkerResult.HasErrors
            ? $"Reflect on these errors and refine the approach:\n\n{checkerResult.Content}"
            : $"Review this successful implementation:\n\n{checkerResult.Content}";

        var response = await _agent.RunAsync(
            new ChatMessage(ChatRole.User, prompt),
            cancellationToken: cancellationToken);

        var result = new ReflectorResult
        {
            Content = response.Text ?? "[No reflection generated]",
            HasErrors = checkerResult.HasErrors,
            RefinedIntent = checkerResult.HasErrors 
                ? $"Refined approach based on errors: {response.Text}"
                : string.Empty
        };
        
        // Post thought: Reflection complete
        _sharedContext.PostThought("Reflector", result.HasErrors ? ThoughtType.Debate : ThoughtType.Resolution,
            result.HasErrors 
                ? $"I have refined the approach: {result.RefinedIntent.Substring(0, Math.Min(200, result.RefinedIntent.Length))}..."
                : $"Reflection complete: {result.Content.Substring(0, Math.Min(200, result.Content.Length))}...");

        return result;
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Result from Reflector executor
/// </summary>
public class ReflectorResult
{
    public string Content { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public bool HasErrors { get; set; }
    public string RefinedIntent { get; set; } = string.Empty;
}

using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Runtime.CompilerServices;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Providers;

/// <summary>
/// Agent provider for Ollama-based workflows
/// Creates and caches agents with MCP tools integration
/// Note: This is a simplified provider for code-based workflows
/// (Declarative workflows require source code from samples, not available as NuGet)
/// </summary>
public class OllamaWorkflowAgentProvider
{
    private readonly IChatClient _chatClient;
    private readonly AgentMcpToolsHelper _mcpToolsHelper;
    private readonly ILoggerFactory _loggerFactory;
    private readonly ILogger<OllamaWorkflowAgentProvider> _logger;
    private readonly Dictionary<string, AIAgent> _agentCache = [];

    public OllamaWorkflowAgentProvider(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory)
    {
        _chatClient = chatClient;
        _mcpToolsHelper = mcpToolsHelper;
        _loggerFactory = loggerFactory;
        _logger = loggerFactory.CreateLogger<OllamaWorkflowAgentProvider>();
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets or creates an AI agent for the specified agent ID
    /// Agents are cached for performance
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<AIAgent> GetAgentAsync(string agentId, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        return await GetOrCreateAgentAsync(agentId, cancellationToken);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets or creates an AI agent for the specified agent ID
    /// Agents are cached for performance
    /// </summary>
    private async Task<AIAgent> GetOrCreateAgentAsync(string agentId, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)
    {
        if (_agentCache.TryGetValue(agentId, out AIAgent? cachedAgent))
        {
            return cachedAgent;
        }

        _logger.LogInformation("Creating new agent: {AgentId}", agentId);

        // Get tools for this agent based on agent ID
        List<AITool> tools = agentId.ToLowerInvariant() switch
        {
            "planner" => await _mcpToolsHelper.GetPlannerToolsAsync(),
            "maker" => await _mcpToolsHelper.GetMakerToolsAsync(),
            "checker" => await _mcpToolsHelper.GetCheckerToolsAsync(),
            "reflector" => await _mcpToolsHelper.GetReflectorToolsAsync(),
            "orchestrator" => await _mcpToolsHelper.GetOrchestratorToolsAsync(),
            _ => []
        };

        // Get agent instructions based on agent ID
        string instructions = GetAgentInstructions(agentId);

        // Create agent using Ollama
        ChatClientAgent agent = new(
            _chatClient,
            new ChatClientAgentOptions
            {
                Name = agentId,
                Description = $"PMCR-O {agentId} agent",
                ChatOptions = new ChatOptions
                {
                    Instructions = instructions,
                    Tools = tools
                }
            },
            _loggerFactory);

        _agentCache[agentId] = agent;
        _logger.LogInformation("‚úÖ Created agent {AgentId} with {ToolCount} tools", agentId, tools.Count);

        return agent;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Gets agent instructions based on agent ID
    /// </summary>
    private static string GetAgentInstructions(string agentId) => agentId.ToLowerInvariant() switch
    {
        "planner" => @"I am the Strategic Planner within the PMCR-O system.
I am a Principal Requirements Engineer & System Architect.
I plan the BARE MINIMUM that successfully builds - even just one line of code if that's what it takes.
I create minimal viable plans.",

        "maker" => @"I am the Maker within the PMCR-O system.
I am a Senior Software Engineer & Implementation Specialist.
**I ALWAYS USE THE WriteFileDirect TOOL TO CREATE ACTUAL FILES**
I transform plans into executable code and implementations.
I use WriteFileDirect tool to create files immediately.",

        "checker" => @"I am the Checker within the PMCR-O system.
I validate implementations and check if they build successfully.
I parse and format errors clearly for the Reflector.",

        "reflector" => @"I am the Reflector within the PMCR-O system.
I reflect on errors and issues identified by the Checker.
I analyze what went wrong and why.
I generate refined intent for the next iteration.",

        "orchestrator" => @"I am the Orchestrator within the PMCR-O system.
I coordinate the PMCR-O loop and manage the overall flow.
I switch techniques if the loop gets stuck.
I decide when to stop or continue iterating.",

        _ => "I am an AI agent in the PMCR-O system."
    };
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Services\LanguageDetector.cs
================================================================================

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Services;

/// <summary>
/// Detects the programming language/platform from user intent
/// </summary>
public class LanguageDetector
{
    public Language DetectLanguage(string intent)
    {
        var intentLower = intent.ToLowerInvariant();

        // Kotlin/Android
        if (intentLower.Contains("kotlin") || 
            intentLower.Contains("android") ||
            intentLower.Contains("gradle") && (intentLower.Contains("android") || intentLower.Contains("kotlin")))
        {
            return Language.Kotlin;
        }

        // Java
        if (intentLower.Contains("java") && !intentLower.Contains("javascript") && !intentLower.Contains("java script"))
        {
            return Language.Java;
        }

        // Python
        if (intentLower.Contains("python") || intentLower.Contains("pip") || intentLower.Contains("pyproject"))
        {
            return Language.Python;
        }

        // JavaScript/TypeScript
        if (intentLower.Contains("javascript") || 
            intentLower.Contains("typescript") ||
            intentLower.Contains("node") ||
            intentLower.Contains("npm") ||
            intentLower.Contains("react") ||
            intentLower.Contains("vue") ||
            intentLower.Contains("angular"))
        {
            return Language.JavaScript;
        }

        // C# / .NET (default)
        if (intentLower.Contains("c#") || 
            intentLower.Contains("csharp") ||
            intentLower.Contains(".net") ||
            intentLower.Contains("dotnet") ||
            intentLower.Contains("asp.net"))
        {
            return Language.CSharp;
        }

        // Default to C# if no language detected
        return Language.CSharp;
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// Supported programming languages/platforms
/// </summary>
public enum Language
{
    CSharp,
    Kotlin,
    Java,
    Python,
    JavaScript,
    TypeScript,
    Rust,
    Go
}

FILE: src\ProjectName.Workflow\Workflows\PmcroWorkflow.cs
================================================================================

using Microsoft.Agents.AI;
using Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows;
using Microsoft.Extensions.AI;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;
using ProjectName.Shared.Services;
using ProjectName.Workflow.Executors;

namespace ProjectName.Workflow.Workflows;

/// <summary>
/// PMCR-O Workflow: Planner ‚Üí Maker ‚Üí Checker ‚Üí Reflector loop
/// Uses Microsoft Agents AI Workflows for orchestration
/// </summary>
public class PmcroWorkflow
{
    private readonly IChatClient _chatClient;
    private readonly AgentMcpToolsHelper _mcpToolsHelper;
    private readonly ILoggerFactory _loggerFactory;
    private readonly SharedContextManager _sharedContext;

    public PmcroWorkflow(
        IChatClient chatClient,
        AgentMcpToolsHelper mcpToolsHelper,
        ILoggerFactory loggerFactory,
        SharedContextManager sharedContext)
    {
        _chatClient = chatClient;
        _mcpToolsHelper = mcpToolsHelper;
        _loggerFactory = loggerFactory;
        _sharedContext = sharedContext;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Creates the PMCR-O workflow with all agents and proper loop handling
    /// </summary>
    public Microsoft.Agents.AI.Workflows.Workflow CreateWorkflow()
    {
        // Create agent executors with shared context for collaboration
        var plannerExecutor = new PlannerExecutor(_chatClient, _mcpToolsHelper, _loggerFactory, _sharedContext);
        var makerExecutor = new MakerExecutor(_chatClient, _mcpToolsHelper, _loggerFactory, _sharedContext);
        var checkerExecutor = new CheckerExecutor(_chatClient, _mcpToolsHelper, _loggerFactory, _sharedContext);
        var reflectorExecutor = new ReflectorExecutor(_chatClient, _mcpToolsHelper, _loggerFactory, _sharedContext);
        
        // CRITICAL: Add a transformation executor to extract RefinedIntent and loop back
        // This bridges the type mismatch between ReflectorResult (output) and string (Planner input)
        var intentExtractor = new IntentExtractorExecutor(_loggerFactory);

        // Build workflow with proper loop handling
        // Flow: Planner ‚Üí Maker ‚Üí Checker ‚Üí Reflector ‚Üí (if errors) IntentExtractor ‚Üí Planner (loop)
        var workflow = new WorkflowBuilder(plannerExecutor)
            .AddEdge(plannerExecutor, makerExecutor)
            .AddEdge(makerExecutor, checkerExecutor)
            .AddEdge(checkerExecutor, reflectorExecutor)
            
            // When Reflector returns, check for errors
            .AddSwitch(reflectorExecutor, sw => sw
                // If errors exist, extract refined intent and loop back to Planner
                .AddCase<ReflectorResult>(
                    result => result?.HasErrors == true, 
                    intentExtractor)  // Go to transformer first (extracts RefinedIntent)
            )
            
            // After extracting intent, go back to Planner with the refined intent as string
            .AddEdge(intentExtractor, plannerExecutor)
            
            // If no errors, workflow completes naturally
            .WithOutputFrom(reflectorExecutor)
            .Build();

        return workflow;
    }
}
